              As Tiga Healthcare Technologies, with our human-centered vision and our proactive, solution-focused approach, we develop national-scale health informatics solutions and drug tracking &amp; tracing technologies. Thanks to our health informatics solutions that focus on sensitive health data management, patient safety and data analysis, we touch the lives of millions of people as pioneers in healthcare digitalization. 

With our healthcare solutions for interoperable systems, patient engagement, drug management, drug traceability and public health informatics, we tirelessly work to create an analyzable, sustainable and developable health ecosystem. In our proven projects, we adopt a patient-centered perspective and move forward with an innovative vision that continuously improves itself. Through our solutions, we provide benefits to individuals, society, public authorities and healthcare regulators, leading the way in health informatics.

          Uzmanlık Alanları
      </dt>
      <dd class="font-sans px-0.25 text-md text-color-text break-words overflow-hidden">
        
                  Healthcare Interoperability, Pharmaceutical Track and Trace System, Patient Engagement, Healthcare Technologies, Healthcare IT, Population Health Management, Electronic Medical Record Systems, Electronic Health Record Systems, e-Health, Personal Health Record Systems, Drug Traceability, Pharma Management, Personalized Healthcare, Hospital Information Systems ve Health Analytics

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">According to the <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/world-health-organization?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>World Health Organization</a>, by 2030 one in six people worldwide will be aged 60 years or older. This projection highlights the importance of the International Day of Older Persons, which reflects the critical need to support aging populations via innovative solutions.  

Our data-driven systems empower healthcare providers and professionals to deliver seamless, integrated care for older adults. By promoting comprehensive and personalized insights, we create stronger health ecosystems adapting to aging populations’ needs and demands.  

Further information from the WHO: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/gTvs78M?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/gTvs78M</a>  

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Ftiga&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Tiga</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fhealthcareit&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#HealthcareIT</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Finternationaldayofolderpersons&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#InternationalDayofOlderPersons</a> </p>

        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">44 of 53 Member States of <a class="link" href="https://ch.linkedin.com/company/world-health-organization?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>World Health Organization</a> Europe Region have a national digital health policy or strategy, and 43 of them prioritize interoperability as a key component of their initiatives. Addressing this need calls for Tiga Healthcare Technologies’ vision and innovation! 

Our interoperability solutions, referred to as HIE Suite, enable different healthcare systems to securely exchange information and collaborate without barriers. With our technologies, we transform fragmented data into a unified, connected ecosystem.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">On World Pharmacists Day, we appreciate the pivotal role pharmacists play in shaping healthier communities. By bridging the gap between prescribers and patients, they not only dispense medications but also ensure safe and appropriate medication use.  

Our e-Pharmacy System continuously supports pharmacists by managing pharmacy workflows such as drug refill requests, stock checking, and insurance payments. This technology performs the necessary dispensing controls and provides pharmacists with real-time alerts and updates, helping to reduce workload and prevent burnout. 

Explore e-Pharmacy: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dV9w7-bn?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dV9w7-bn</a>

        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Drug safety ensures that medications provide the intended benefits without causing harmful side effects or dangerous interactions. Our award-winning Pharmaceutical Track &amp; Trace System, DrugXafe, acts as the invisible guardian of pharmaceutical supply chains, preventing counterfeit or substandard medicines from reaching patients. In this way, it safeguards both drug integrity and patient safety. 

Let’s shape the future together with end-to-end drug tracking and tracing!

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">We asked our Business Analyst, Naciye Kürük Durmaz, “What are the key benefits of the seamless integration of different health information systems?”. She expresses that seamless integration guarantees data flow between diverse systems, eased workflows, and secure access to patient health records. In brief, integration is not merely a technical convenience; it enhances efficiency and quality of care. 

Our Personal Health Record (PHR) System is integrated with more than 40 systems, including e-Appointment, Central e-Prescription, and EMPI. This reflects our commitment to make healthcare ecosystem patient-centric and unified via seamless data exchange.
